0MEMORYADDR0 ; RAM definitions

0MEMORYADDR0 ; Note: The system RAM maps in at 0080-00FF and also at 0180-01FF. It is

0MEMORYADDR0 ; used for variables and the system stack. The programmer must make sure

0MEMORYADDR0 ; the stack never grows so deep as to overwrite the variables.

0MEMORYADDR0 ; RAM definitions

0MEMORYADDR0 ; Note: The system RAM maps in at 0080-00FF and also at 0180-01FF. It is

0MEMORYADDR0 ; used for variables and the system stack. The programmer must make sure

0MEMORYADDR0 ; the stack never grows so deep as to overwrite the variables.

0MEMORYADDR0 ;
